I wanted a large size bathrobe, but it was available the day before, and I was told that it was out of stock the next day. In fact, I have been used to staying here every time I come to Bayuquan for many years, but I hope the store can improve these small details. The most important thing is that I used to stay in a deluxe sea view room every time I went there, and there were wooden hangers in the room, but this time there were none, which made it inconvenient to hang the washed clothes. I asked the waiter for one, and the room service brought one and told me that only suites are equipped with this hanger now, and general rooms are not equipped with it, because some are broken and not enough. I was really speechless. I originally lived here for the convenience of living. A clothes hanger is not worth much money. If it is gone, just make up for it. This thing is only available in suites. If it is like this next time, I will definitely not stay here, and I will stay in Wanda. The buffet dishes are really not delicious. There is a limited amount of fried chicken popcorn. If you go late, there will be no more, and they will not be replenished. There is only instant coffee in the coffee machine, not even a freshly ground black coffee machine. Bananas are cut in half. The water in the hot spring pool is not very clear. The shower head is OK, but the shower head is not easy to use and sprays water everywhere. Although the beach outside is not a closed private beach, I hope the hotel can send people to clean up the beach and the garbage washed up by the sea. After all, half of the reason for coming to your house is to go to the beach. The hotel has put more and more kiosks and huts on the beach to sell things, but it seems that no one patronizes them, and it also affects the overall beauty and greatly affects the mood of watching the sea when staying here. There is a Best Cola vending machine in the middle of the road leading to the beach, which is quite annoying. I donâ€™t know how much money this thing can generate for the hotel. Anyway, the experience has been worse and worse in the past two years. I remember that it was very good when I came here five or six years ago. Anyway, the store owner should improve it himself, or I will not stay here in the future.
